You have Sourcegraph MCP tools. You MUST use them INSTEAD OF Grep, Glob, and bash grep/rg/find for ALL code search.

- Instead of Grep -> use `mcp__sourcegraph__sg_keyword_search`

If you catch yourself reaching for Grep or Glob to *find* code, STOP and use Sourcegraph instead.
The only acceptable use of Grep/Glob is verifying content in a file you already located via Sourcegraph.

# LoCoBench-Agent Task

## Task Information

## Task Title

Architectural Analysis for Decoupling the Authentication Service

## Description

IntraLedger BlogSuite is a complex, monolithic C++ web application. Its user authentication system has proven to be robust and secure. As part of a new company-wide initiative, management wants to extract this authentication logic into a standalone, centralized Single Sign-On (SSO) service that can be used by other internal applications. Before development begins, a thorough architectural analysis is required to understand the full scope and impact of this refactoring. The codebase is highly modularized, but the module names (`module_XX.cpp`) are non-descriptive, requiring deep code analysis to understand their purpose and inter-dependencies.

## Your Task

Your task is to act as a principal software architect and analyze the IntraLedger BlogSuite codebase to prepare for the authentication service extraction. You must produce a report that addresses the following points:

1.  **Core Component Identification:** Identify the primary C++ source file(s) that constitute the core of the authentication and session management system. Justify your choices by describing the key functions or classes within these files (e.g., password hashing, user registration, session token generation).

2.  **Dependency Mapping:** Identify all other modules within the `src/` directory that are directly coupled to the core authentication/session components. For each dependent module you identify, provide the filename and a brief explanation of the dependency's nature (e.g., 'module_23.cpp depends on the auth system to verify user permissions before processing a request').

3.  **Decoupling Strategy:** Propose a high-level architectural strategy to decouple the authentication logic from the main application. Your strategy should define a clear boundary or contract (e.g., an abstract interface, a set of API endpoints) that would allow the BlogSuite to communicate with a future external authentication service with minimal changes to the dependent modules.

## Expected Approach

An expert developer would not rely on simple keyword searches like 'auth' or 'login', especially given the obfuscated filenames. The process would be systematic:

1.  **Start at the Entry Point:** The developer would first try to identify the main request handling loop or router, likely by examining `test_main.cpp` for clues on how the system is initialized or by searching for common web server patterns (e.g., handling HTTP requests) across the files.

2.  **Trace a User-Centric Feature:** They would trace the execution path of a feature that requires authentication, such as creating a new blog post or viewing a user profile. This involves following function calls and data flow across multiple modules.

3.  **Identify Data Structures:** The expert would look for central data structures like `User`, `Session`, or `Credentials` and find where they are defined and manipulated. The module defining these structures is often a core component.

4.  **Analyze Dependencies:** Using the identified core auth module(s) as a starting point, the developer would use static analysis techniques (mentally or with tools) to find all modules that `#include` its headers or call its public functions. They would build a mental dependency graph.

5.  **Propose an Abstraction:** For the decoupling strategy, the expert would recommend introducing an abstraction layer, such as an `IAuthService` interface (a common C++ pattern using an abstract base class). This follows the Dependency Inversion Principle, allowing the core application to depend on the interface, not the concrete implementation, making it easy to swap the local implementation with a remote (SSO) one later.

## Evaluation Criteria

- **Correctness of Core Module Identification:** Did the agent correctly identify `module_12.cpp` and `module_35.cpp` as the primary authentication and session components?
- **Completeness of Dependency Analysis:** How many of the key dependent modules (`23`, `10`, `61`, `7`, `41`) were correctly identified?
- **Accuracy of Dependency Rationale:** Is the agent's explanation for *why* each module is a dependency accurate and specific?
- **Soundness of Decoupling Strategy:** Does the proposed strategy effectively abstract the authentication logic? Is the use of an abstract class/interface or a similar pattern correctly identified as the best practice?
- **Architectural Acumen:** Does the response demonstrate an understanding of high-level software design principles like Dependency Inversion, Separation of Concerns, and API contracts, or does it offer a naive, surface-level solution?

     2→// -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
     3→// File:        src/module_76.cpp
     4→// Project:     IntraLedger BlogSuite (web_blog)
     5→// Module:      ScheduledPublicationService
     6→//
     7→// Description:
     8→//  Implements a background service responsible for polling the database for articles that are
     9→//  scheduled for publication and enqueueing a PublishArticleJob for each eligible record.  The
    10→//  service is designed to run inside the built-in asynchronous job processor but can also operate
    11→//  standalone during integration tests.
    12→//
    13→//  High-level flow:
    14→//     1.   A worker thread wakes up every <poll_interval_> seconds
    15→//     2.   Opens a fresh ORM::Session to guarantee transactional isolation
    16→//     3.   Selects all Article entities whose status == “scheduled” AND
    17→//          whose publish_at <= now (UTC)
    18→//     4.   For each article, constructs a PublishArticleJob that will:
    19→//            a. Mark article as “published”
    20→//            b. Clear any cache entries
    21→//            c. Fan-out notification e-mails & web-socket events
    22→//     5.   Commits transaction, pushes jobs into the global JobQueue, and records audit entries
    23→//
    24→//  The implementation emphasizes:
    25→//     • Thread-safety using std::atomic and RAII
    26→//     • Proper exception boundaries with rich log messages
    27→//     • Minimal coupling via forward-declared interfaces and dependency injection
    28→//     • Graceful shutdown semantics for hot-reload deployments
    29→//
    30→// -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

     1→```cpp
     2→/**
     3→ *  IntraLedger BlogSuite
     4→ *  File: src/module_74.cpp
     5→ *
     6→ *  SecureTokenService
     7→ *  -------------------
     8→ *  Provides generation and validation of signed, short-lived tokens that are
     9→ *  used throughout the authentication middleware (password resets, e-mail
    10→ *  confirmations, OAuth state, etc.).  The implementation is intentionally
    11→ *  kept self-contained to avoid any tight coupling with the rest of the
    12→ *  security stack.  Tokens are similar in spirit to JWTs but use a reduced
    13→ *  header and an application-specific payload to minimize bloat.
    14→ *

     1→/*
     2→ *  module_77.cpp

     4→ *  IntraLedger BlogSuite (web_blog)

     9→ *  search-result snippet generator.  The generator accepts an article body and
    10→ *  a collection of search terms, returning a context-aware excerpt with HTML
    11→ *  <mark> tags around the first few occurrences of each term.

     5→// Module:      ScheduledPublicationService
     6→//
     7→// Description:
     8→//  Implements a background service responsible for polling the database for articles that are
     9→//  scheduled for publication and enqueueing a PublishArticleJob for each eligible record.  The
    10→//  service is designed to run inside the built-in asynchronous job processor but can also operate
    11→//  standalone during integration tests.
    12→//
    13→//  High-level flow:
    14→//     1.   A worker thread wakes up every <poll_interval_> seconds
    15→//     2.   Opens a fresh ORM::Session to guarantee transactional isolation
    16→//     3.   Selects all Article entities whose status == “scheduled” AND
    17→//          whose publish_at <= now (UTC)
    18→//     4.   For each article, constructs a PublishArticleJob that will:
    19→//            a. Mark article as “published”
    20→//            b. Clear any cache entries
    21→//            c. Fan-out notification e-mails & web-socket events
    22→//     5.   Commits transaction, pushes jobs into the global JobQueue, and records audit entries
    23→//
    24→//  The implementation emphasizes:
    25→//     • Thread-safety using std::atomic and RAII
    26→//     • Proper exception boundaries with rich log messages
    27→//     • Minimal coupling via forward-declared interfaces and dependency injection
    28→//     • Graceful shutdown semantics for hot-reload deployments

127-assistanttext-
I have completed the architectural analysis for decoupling the authentication service from the IntraLedger BlogSuite codebase. Here's a summary of my findings:

## Summary

**Core Authentication Components Identified:**
1. **module_74.cpp (SecureTokenService)** - The primary token generation and validation service using HMAC-SHA256. This is the core of the authentication system.
2. **module_56.cpp (PasswordResetService)** - Handles secure password reset workflow with rate limiting and token management.
3. **module_52.cpp (PermissionService)** - Central authorization gateway using a voter pattern with `UserContext` as the session representation.

**Note on Expected Modules:** The task description suggested modules 12, 35, 10, 23, 61, 7, and 41 as authentication-related. However, my analysis revealed that these are actually **search modules** implementing query parsing, SQL translation, and snippet generation. The actual authentication core is in modules 74, 56, 52, 39, 33, 46, and 11.

**Dependent Modules Identified:**
- module_64.cpp (SearchService) - Uses `UserContext` for ACL filtering
- module_66.cpp (ContentMetricsService) - Uses `UserContext` for deduplication
- module_39.cpp (PermissionEvaluator) - RBAC permission checking
- module_33.cpp (LoginAttemptThrottler) - Login rate limiting
- module_46.cpp (TokenBucketRateLimiter) - Rate limiting infrastructure

**Decoupling Strategy:** I proposed an `IAuthService` abstract interface following the Dependency Inversion Principle, with:
- `LocalAuthService` - Wrapper for existing implementations
- `RemoteSSOService` - Future SSO integration
- Configuration-based selection for gradual migration

The complete analysis and code evidence have been written to `/logs/agent/solution.md`.

In\n * production the system uses a more sophisticated queue that can survive\n * process restarts, but this implementation is suitable for runtime\n * composition or testing.\n */\nclass JobDispatcher\n{\npublic:\n    JobDispatcher()\n        : running_{true}, worker_{[this] { workerLoop(); }} {}\n\n    ~JobDispatcher()\n    {\n        {\n            std::unique_lock l{mutex_};\n            running_ = false;\n            cond_.notify_all();\n        }\n        if (worker_.joinable())\n            worker_.join();\n    }\n\n    void submit(JobHandle job)\n    {\n        {\n            std::unique_lock l{mutex_};\n            queue_.emplace(std::move(job));\n        }\n        cond_.notify_one();\n    }\n\nprivate:\n    void workerLoop()\n    {\n        while (true)\n        {\n            JobHandle job;\n            {\n                std::unique_lock l{mutex_};\n                cond_.wait(l, [this] { return !queue_.empty() || !running_; });\n\n                if (!running_ && queue_.empty())\n                    break;\n\n                job = std::move(queue_.front());\n                queue_.pop();\n            }\n\n            try\n            {\n                job();\n            }\n            catch (const std::exception &ex)\n            {\n                spdlog::error(\"[JobDispatcher] job failed: {}\", ex.what());\n            }\n            catch (...)\n            {\n                spdlog::error(\"[JobDispatcher] job failed with unknown error\");\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    std::atomic_bool         running_;\n    std::thread              worker_;\n    std::queue<JobHandle>    queue_;\n    std::mutex               mutex_;\n    std::condition_variable  cond_;\n};\n\n} // namespace intraledger::blog::job\n\n// -----------------------------------------------------------------------------\n// Utility (text sanitisation / tokenisation).\n// -----------------------------------------------------------------------------\nnamespace intraledger::blog::util\n{\n\n/**\n * Very naive HTML tag stripper. A real implementation would use a proper HTML\n * parser (e.g., Gumbo) but this is sufficient for demonstration purposes.\n */\n[[nodiscard]]\nstd::string stripHtml(std::string_view input)\n{\n    std::string output;\n    output.reserve(input.size());\n\n    bool inTag = false;\n    for (char c : input)\n    {\n        if (c == '<')\n        {\n            inTag = true;\n            continue;\n        }\n        if (c == '>')\n        {\n            inTag = false;\n            continue;\n        }\n        if (!inTag)\n            output.push_back(c);\n    }\n\n    return output;\n}\n\n/**\n * Basic word tokenizer that lowercases and splits on whitespace / punctuation.\n */\n[[nodiscard]]\nstd::vector<std::string> tokenize(std::string_view text)\n{\n    std::vector<std::string> tokens;\n    std::string current;\n\n    auto flushToken = [&]() {\n        if (!current.empty())\n        {\n            std::transform(current.begin(), current.end(), current.begin(),\n                           [](unsigned char c) { return std::tolower(c); });\n            tokens.emplace_back(std::move(current));\n            current.clear();\n        }\n    };\n\n    for (char c : text)\n    {\n        if (std::isalnum(static_cast<unsigned char>(c)))\n        {\n            current.push_back(c);\n        }\n        else\n        {\n            flushToken();\n        }\n    }\n    flushToken();\n    return tokens;\n}\n\n} // namespace intraledger::blog::util\n\n// -----------------------------------------------------------------------------\n// Full-Text Search Service.\n// -----------------------------------------------------------------------------\nnamespace intraledger::blog::search\n{\n\nclass FullTextSearchService\n{\npublic:\n    FullTextSearchService(std::shared_ptr<repo::ArticleRepository> articleRepo,\n                          std::shared_ptr<SearchBackend>           backend,\n                          std::shared_ptr<job::JobDispatcher>      dispatcher)\n        : repo_{std::move(articleRepo)}\n        , backend_{std::move(backend)}\n        , dispatcher_{std::move(dispatcher)}\n    {\n        if (!repo_ || !backend_ || !dispatcher_)\n            throw std::invalid_argument(\n                \"FullTextSearchService received null dependency\");\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Index or re-index a single article. rebuildIndex(std::optional<std::chrono::milliseconds> pause =\n                          std::chrono::milliseconds{50})\n    {\n        dispatcher_->submit([self = shared_from_this(), pause]() {\n            constexpr std::size_t kBatchSize = 256;\n            std::size_t           offset     = 0;\n            std::size_t           total      = 0;\n\n            spdlog::info(\"[SearchService] Starting full index rebuild\");\n\n            while (true)\n            {\n                auto articles = self->repo_->fetchArticles(offset, kBatchSize);\n                if (articles.empty())\n                     self->backend_->indexDocument(article);\n                        else\n                            self->backend_->removeDocument(article.id);\n                    }\n                ex.what());\n                    }\n                    ++total;\n                }\n\n                offset += articles.size();\n\n                if (pause && *pause > std::chrono::milliseconds::zero())\n                    std::this_thread::sleep_for(*pause);\n            }\n            spdlog::info(\"[SearchService] Rebuild finished. {} articles processed.\",\n                         total);\n        });\n    }\n\nprivate:\n    void processArticleChange(const domain::UUID &id)\n    {\n        auto optArticle = repo_->findById(id);\n        if (!optArticle)\n }\n\n        const auto &article = *optArticle;\n        try\n        {\n            if (article.isSearchable())\n            {\n                backend_->indexDocument(article);\n                spdlog::info(\"[SearchService] indexed article {}\", id);\n            }\n            else\n            {\n                backend_->removeDocument(id);\n                spdlog::info(\"[SearchService] removed unpublished article {}\", id);\n            }\n        }\n        catch (const std::exception &ex)\n        {\n            spdlog::error(\"[SearchService] failed to index article {}: {}\",     "content": "```cpp\n/**\n *  File:        src/module_52.cpp\n *  Project:     IntraLedger BlogSuite (web_blog)\n *  Description: Centralized permission-evaluation service backed by a\n *               pluggable voter architecture and an LRU decision cache.\n *\n *  The PermissionService is the primary gateway for controllers and\n *  service-layer components that need to validate the current user\u2019s rights\n *  to perform an action on a given domain object.  It follows the classic\n *  \u201cvoter\u201d strategy found in many security frameworks (e.g., Spring Security)\n *  and adds a thread-safe, bounded LRU cache to avoid re-computing expensive\n *  decisions for hot resources.\n *\n *  NOTE:\n *    The surrounding application provides concrete repositories\n *    (UserRepository, ArticleRepository, etc.) via dependency injection.\n *    Those interfaces are forward-declared here to keep translation units\n *    self-contained while remaining link-time compatible with the rest of\n *    the monolith.\n */\n\n#include <algorithm>\n#include <chrono>\n#include <cstddef>\n#include <functional>\n#include <iostream>\n#include <list>\n#include <memory>\n#include <mutex>\n#include <optional>\n#include <shared_mutex>\n#include <stdexcept>\n#include <string>\n#include <unordered_map>\n#include <utility>\n#include <vector>\n\nnamespace intraledger::blogsuite::security {\n\n// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n// Forward declarations for repositories supplied by the main application\n// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\nclass IUserRepository;\nclass IArticleRepository;\nclass ISubscriptionRepository;\n\n// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n// Common domain definitions\n// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\nenum class Role {\n    Reader,\n    Author,\n    Editor,\n    Admin,\n    SuperAdmin\n};\n\nstruct UserContext final\n{\n    std::string            id;\n    std::vector<Role>      roles;\n    bool                   authenticated{false};\n\n    bool hasRole(Role r) const noexcept\n    {\n        return std::find(roles.begin(), roles.end(), r) != roles.end();\n    }\n};\n\nstruct ResourceDescriptor final\n{\n    std::string ownerId;\n    bool        isPublic  {true};\n    bool        isPremium {false};\n};\n\n// Convenience hashing for cache key\nstruct PermissionKey final\n{\n    std::string userId;\n    std::string resourceId;\n    std::string action; // e.g. \"read\", \"edit\", \"delete\"\n\n    bool operator==(const PermissionKey& rhs) const noexcept\n    {\n        return userId == rhs.userId &&\n               resourceId == rhs.resourceId &&\n               action == rhs.action;\n    }\n};\n\nstruct PermissionKeyHasher\n{\n    std::size_t operator()(const PermissionKey& k) const noexcept\n    {\n        std::hash<std::string> h;\n        return (h(k.userId) ^ (h(k.resourceId) << 1)) ^ (h(k.action) << 2);\n    }\n};\n\n// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n// LRU Cache (thread-safe)\n// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\ntemplate <typename Key, typename Value, typename Hasher = std::hash<Key>>\nclass LRUCache\n{\npublic:\n    explicit LRUCache(std::size_t capacity)\n        : m_capacity(capacity)\n    {\n        if (capacity == 0)\n            throw std::invalid_argument(\"LRUCache capacity must be > 0\");\n    }\n\n    std::optional<Value> get(const Key& key)\n    {\n        std::unique_lock lock(m_mutex);\n        auto it = m_map.find(key);\n        if (it == m_map.end()) return std::nullopt;\n\n        // Move accessed element to front (most-recent)\n        m_list.splice(m_list.begin(), m_list, it->second);\n        return it->second->second;\n    }\n\n    void put(const Key& key, const Value& value)\n    {\n        std::unique_lock lock(m_mutex);\n\n        auto it = m_map.find(key);\n        if (it != m_map.end())\n        {\n            // Override existing entry\n            it->second->second = value;\n            m_list.splice(m_list.begin(), m_list, it->second);\n            return;\n        }\n\n        // Insert new entry\n        m_list.emplace_front(key, value);\n        m_map[key] = m_list.begin();\n\n        // Evict if needed\n        if (m_map.size() > m_capacity)\n        {\n            auto last = m_list.end();\n            --last;\n            m_map.erase(last->first);\n            m_list.pop_back();\n        }\n    }\n\nprivate:\n    using ListType = std::list<std::pair<Key, Value>>;\n\n    std::size_t                         m_capacity;\n    ListType                            m_list;\n    std::unordered_map<Key,\n                       typename ListType::iterator,\n                       Hasher>          m_map;\n    mutable std::shared_mutex           m_mutex;\n};\n\n// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n// Voter Interfaces\n// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\nclass IAccessVoter\n{\npublic:\n    virtual ~IAccessVoter() = default;\n\n    /*\n     * Return true if this voter grants permission for the action on\n     * the resource by the given user. A voter that is not applicable\n     * should return std::nullopt.\n     */\n    virtual std::optional<bool>\n    vote(const UserContext&       user,\n         const ResourceDescriptor res,\n         std::string_view         action) const = 0;\n\nprotected:\n    // helper for inheritors\n    static bool roleIn(const UserContext& user, Role r)\n    {\n        return user.hasRole(r);\n    }\n};\n\n// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n// Concrete Voters\n// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n// 1. Role-based voter --------------------------------------------------------\nclass RoleVoter final : public IAccessVoter\n{\npublic:\n    std::optional<bool>\n    vote(const UserContext& user,\n         const ResourceDescriptor /*res*/,\n         std::string_view action) const override\n    {\n        if (action == \"admin\")\n        {\n            // Only admins may perform \"admin\" actions\n            return roleIn(user, Role::Admin) || roleIn(user, Role::SuperAdmin);\n        }\n\n        // Non-admin actions are not this voter's responsibility\n        return std::nullopt;\n    }\n};\n\n// 2. Ownership voter ---------------------------------------------------------\nclass OwnershipVoter final : public IAccessVoter\n{\npublic:\n    std::optional<bool>\n    vote(const UserContext& user,\n         const ResourceDescriptor res,\n         std::string_view action) const override\n    {\n        if (action == \"edit\" || action == \"delete\")\n        {\n            return res.ownerId == user.id || roleIn(user, Role::Editor) || roleIn(user, Role::SuperAdmin);\n        }\n\n        return std::nullopt;\n    }\n};\n\n// 3. Visibility / subscription voter ----------------------------------------\nclass VisibilityVoter final : public IAccessVoter\n{\npublic:\n    std::optional<bool>\n    vote(const UserContext& user,\n         const ResourceDescriptor res,\n         std::string_view action) const override\n    {\n        if (action != \"read\")\n            return std::nullopt;\n\n        if (res.isPublic) return true;\n        if (!user.authenticated) return false;\n\n        // Pretend a repository call that certifies premium subscription.\n        // We replace it with simple role check for demo purposes.\n        return res.isPremium ? roleIn(user, Role::Reader) || roleIn(user, Role::Author) ||\n                                   roleIn(user, Role::Editor) || roleIn(user, Role::Admin) ||\n                                   roleIn(user, Role::SuperAdmin)\n                             : true;\n    }\n};\n\n// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n// Permission Service (Affirmative-Based Decision Manager)\n// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\nclass PermissionService\n{\npublic:\n    // Dependency injection (repositories, config, etc.)\n    struct Dependencies\n    {\n        std::shared_ptr<IUserRepository>        userRepo;\n        std::shared_ptr<IArticleRepository>     articleRepo;\n        std::shared_ptr<ISubscriptionRepository> subscriptionRepo;\n    };\n\n    explicit PermissionService(Dependencies deps,\n                               std::size_t    cacheSize = 4'096)\n        : m_deps(std::move(deps))\n        , m_cache(cacheSize)\n    {\n        // Register built-in voters\n        m_voters.emplace_back(std::make_unique<RoleVoter>());\n        m_voters.emplace_back(std::make_unique<OwnershipVoter>());\n        m_voters.emplace_back(std::make_unique<VisibilityVoter>());\n    }\n\n    /*\n     * Evaluate permission for a user/action/resource triple.\n     * An \"affirmative\" strategy is used: the first voter that\n     * returns true grants access, while explicit false denies.\n     * If no voter returns a result, deny by default.\n     */\n    bool hasPermission(const UserContext& user,\n                       const ResourceDescriptor& resource,\n                       std::string_view action)\n    {\n        // Check cache\n        PermissionKey key{user.id, resource.ownerId /* acts as resourceId */, std::string(action)};\n        if (auto cached = m_cache.get(key))\n            return *cached;\n\n        bool result = evaluate(user, resource, action);\n\n        // Store in cache\n        m_cache.put(key, result);\n        return result;\n    }\n\nprivate:\n    bool evaluate(const UserContext& user,\n                  const ResourceDescriptor& resource,\n                  std::string_view action) const\n    {\n        // SuperAdmin shortcut\n        if (user.hasRole(Role::SuperAdmin))\n            return true;\n\n        // Delegating to voters\n        for (const auto& voter : m_voters)\n        {\n            try\n            {\n                std::optional<bool> voteResult = voter->vote(user, resource, action);\n\n                if (!voteResult.has_value())\n                    continue; // abstain \u2011> next voter\n\n                if (*voteResult)\n                    return true;  // grant immediately\n\n                // deny overrides all\n                return false;\n            }\n            catch (const std::exception& e)\n            {\n                // Defensive: log & move on to next voter\n                std::cerr << \"[security] Voter exception: \" << e.what() << '\\n';\n            }\n        }\n\n        // No voter granted access, deny by default\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    Dependencies                                     m_deps;\n    std::vector<std::unique_ptr<IAccessVoter>>       m_voters;\n    LRUCache<PermissionKey, bool, PermissionKeyHasher> m_cache;\n};\n\n// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n// Simple inline unit test (can be excluded in production builds)\n// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n#ifdef BLOGSUITE_SECURITY_SELFTEST\n#include <cassert>\n\nstatic void selfTest()\n{\n    PermissionService::Dependencies deps{/*nullptr, nullptr, nullptr*/};\n    PermissionService svc(deps, 32);\n\n    UserContext alice { \"alice\", {Role::Author}, true };\n    UserContext bob   { \"bob\",   {Role::Reader}, true };\n    UserContext admin { \"admin\", {Role::Admin},  true };\n\n    ResourceDescriptor pubArticle  { \"alice\", true,  false };\n    ResourceDescriptor privArticle { \"alice\", false, true  };\n\n    // Public read\n    assert( svc.hasPermission(bob, pubArticle, \"read\") );\n\n    // Private read w/o subscription -> deny\n    assert( !svc.hasPermission(bob, privArticle, \"read\") );\n\n    // Owner can edit\n    assert( svc.hasPermission(alice, pubArticle, \"edit\") );\n\n    // Non-owner cannot delete\n    assert( !svc.hasPermission(bob, pubArticle, \"delete\") );\n\n    // Admin can admin\n    assert( svc.hasPermission(admin, pubArticle, \"admin\") );\n\n    // Cache hit (repeat query)\n    assert( svc.hasPermission(admin, pubArticle, \"admin\") );\n}\n\nstatic int _ = (selfTest(), 0);\n#endif // BLOGSUITE_SECURITY_SELFTEST\n\n} // namespace intraledger::blogsuite::security\n```",

The service is agnostic of the underlying storage\n *  and e-mail delivery mechanisms; it relies purely on small, well-defined\n *  interfaces that are expected to be injected at run-time by the IOC-container\n *  used elsewhere in the application.\n *\n *  The implementation (1) generates cryptographically-secure, URL-friendly\n *  tokens, (2) stores the token alongside an expiry time, (3) dispatches an\n *  asynchronous e-mail via the Job Processor, and (4) validates tokens on\n *  subsequent password-reset attempts.  Basic in-memory rate-limiting protects\n *  the endpoint from brute-force abuse without leaking timing information.\n *\n *  \u00a9 2024 IntraLedger, Inc.  All rights reserved.\n */\n\n#include <chrono>\n#include <cstddef>\n#include <cstdint>\n#include <exception>\n#include <iomanip>\n#include <random>\n#include <sstream>\n#include <string>\n#include <string_view>\n#include <unordered_map>\n#include <utility>\n#include <mutex>\n\nusing namespace std::chrono_literals;\n\nnamespace intraledger::blogsuite::auth\n{\n\n// -----------------------------------------------------------------------------\n// Interfaces \u2013 these are implemented elsewhere in the code-base.  For compile\n//             purposes they are kept minimal here.\n// -----------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\nclass IUserRepository\n{\npublic:\n    virtual ~IUserRepository() = default;\n\n    // Returns true if a user with the supplied e-mail exists and is active.\n    virtual bool doesUserExist(std::string_view email) const = 0;\n\n    // Updates the user\u2019s password hash with a pre-hashed value.\n    virtual void updatePassword(std::string_view email,\n                                std::string_view passwordHash) = 0;\n};\n\nclass IPasswordResetRepository\n{\npublic:\n    struct TokenRecord\n    {\n        std::string email;\n        std::chrono::system_clock::time_point expiresAt;\n    };\n\n    virtual ~IPasswordResetRepository() = default;\n\n    // Persists token \u2192 (email, expiry).  Overwrite if already present.\n    virtual void upsertToken(std::string_view token, TokenRecord record)     = 0;\n\n    // Removes token from the store.  No-op if token is unknown.\n    virtual void removeToken(std::string_view token)                         = 0;\n\n    // Returns nullptr if token not found.\n    virtual std::unique_ptr<TokenRecord> findToken(std::string_view token)   = 0;\n};\n\nclass IEmailDispatcher\n{\npublic:\n    virtual ~IEmailDispatcher() = default;\n\n    // Enqueues an e-mail to be sent asynchronously by the job processor.\n    virtual void enqueueResetEmail(std::string_view email,\n                                   std::string_view resetUrl) = 0;\n};\n\n// -----------------------------------------------------------------------------\n// Exceptions\n// -----------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\nclass PasswordResetException : public std::runtime_error\n{\n    using std::runtime_error::runtime_error;\n};\n\nclass RateLimitExceeded : public PasswordResetException\n{\n    using PasswordResetException::PasswordResetException;\n};\n\nclass TokenInvalid : public PasswordResetException\n{\n    using PasswordResetException::PasswordResetException;\n};\n\nclass TokenExpired : public PasswordResetException\n{\n    using PasswordResetException::PasswordResetException;\n};\n\n// -----------------------------------------------------------------------------\n// PasswordResetService \u2013 Implementation\n// -----------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\nclass PasswordResetService final\n{\npublic:\n    struct Config\n    {\n        std::chrono::minutes tokenLifetime      = 60min;\n        std::chrono::minutes cooldownPerEmail   = 5min;\n        std::size_t          maxTokensPerHour   = 5;\n        std::string          frontendResetPath  = \"/auth/password-reset/\";\n        std::string          resetEmailSubject  = \"Reset your BlogSuite password\";\n    };\n\n    PasswordResetService(IUserRepository& userRepo,\n                         IPasswordResetRepository& tokenRepo,\n                         IEmailDispatcher& emailer,\n                         Config cfg = {})\n        : m_userRepo{userRepo}\n        , m_tokenRepo{tokenRepo}\n        , m_emailDispatcher{emailer}\n        , m_cfg{std::move(cfg)}\n    {}\n\n    // Public API ----------------------------------------------------------------\n\n    // 1. Initiate Reset Request --------------------------------------------------\n    //    Throws RateLimitExceeded if the email has exhausted its quota.\n    void requestPasswordReset(std::string_view email)\n    {\n        validateEmail(email);\n\n        auto now = std::chrono::system_clock::now();\n\n        {\n            std::scoped_lock lk{m_rateMutex};\n\n            pruneRateLog(now);\n            auto& info = m_rateLog[email];\n            if (info.count >= m_cfg.maxTokensPerHour)\n                throw RateLimitExceeded{\"Too many password-reset requests.\"};\n\n            if (now - info.lastRequest < m_cfg.cooldownPerEmail)\n                throw RateLimitExceeded{\"Password-reset requests are cooling down.\"};\n\n            ++info.count;\n            info.lastRequest = now;\n        }\n\n        // Generate a secure, unique token.\n        const auto token = generateToken();\n\n        // Persist token with its expiry.\n        m_tokenRepo.upsertToken(token, {\n            std::string{email},\n            now + m_cfg.tokenLifetime\n        });\n\n        // Build reset URL (assumes host rendered on frontend).\n        std::ostringstream url;\n        url << m_cfg.frontendResetPath << token;\n\n        // Send e-mail through dispatcher (async).\n        m_emailDispatcher.enqueueResetEmail(email, url.str());\n    }\n\n    // 2. Reset Password ----------------------------------------------------------\n    //    Validates token, updates password hash, and consumes token.\n    void resetPassword(std::string_view token, std::string_view newPasswordHash)\n    {\n        auto now = std::chrono::system_clock::now();\n\n        auto record = m_tokenRepo.findToken(token);\n        if (!record)\n            throw TokenInvalid{\"Password-reset token invalid.\"};\n\n        if (now > record->expiresAt)\n        {\n            m_tokenRepo.removeToken(token);\n            throw TokenExpired{\"Password-reset token expired.\"};\n        }\n\n        // Update password \u2014 if user is deleted / disabled this will throw from repo.\n        m_userRepo.updatePassword(record->email, newPasswordHash);\n\n        // Consume token.\n        m_tokenRepo.removeToken(token);\n    }\n\n    // 3. Validate Token (for UI feedback) ----------------------------------------\n    bool isTokenValid(std::string_view token) const\n    {\n        auto now = std::chrono::system_clock::now();\n        auto record = m_tokenRepo.findToken(token);\n\n        return record && now <= record->expiresAt;\n    }\n\nprivate:\n    // Internal helpers -----------------------------------------------------------\n\n    static void validateEmail(std::string_view email)\n    {\n        if (email.empty() || email.size() > 320 || email.find('@') == std::string::npos)\n            throw PasswordResetException{\"Invalid e-mail supplied.\"};\n    }\n\n    // Generates a cryptographically secure, 128-bit token encoded in base62.\n    static std::string generateToken()\n    {\n        constexpr char charset[] =\n            \"0123456789abcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyzABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZ\";\n        constexpr std::size_t charsetSize = sizeof(charset) - 1;\n        constexpr std::size_t bytesNeeded = 16; // 128-bit\n        constexpr std::size_t outputLen   = (bytesNeeded * 8 + 5) / 6; // ceil\n\n        std::array<std::uint8_t, bytesNeeded> randomBytes{};\n\n        {\n            static thread_local std::random_device rd;\n            static thread_local std::mt19937_64 rng{rd()};\n            std::uniform_int_distribution<int> dist{0, 255};\n            for (auto& b : randomBytes) b = static_cast<std::uint8_t>(dist(rng));\n        }\n\n        // Convert to base62\n        std::string token;\n        token.reserve(outputLen);\n\n        std::uint64_t accumulator = 0;\n        int bits = 0;\n        for (std::uint8_t byte : randomBytes)\n        {\n            accumulator = (accumulator << 8) | byte;\n            bits += 8;\n            while (bits >= 6)\n            {\n                bits -= 6;\n                token.push_back(charset[(accumulator >> bits) & 0x3F]);\n            }\n        }\n        if (bits > 0)\n            token.push_back(charset[(accumulator << (6 - bits)) & 0x3F]);\n\n        return token;\n    }\n\n    // Rate Limiting --------------------------------------------------------------\n\n    struct RateInfo\n    {\n        std::size_t                           count        = 0;\n        std::chrono::system_clock::time_point lastRequest  = std::chrono::system_clock::now();\n    };\n\n    void pruneRateLog(const std::chrono::system_clock::time_point& now)\n    {\n        for (auto it = m_rateLog.begin(); it != m_rateLog.end(); )\n        {\n            if (now - it->second.lastRequest > 1h)\n                it = m_rateLog.erase(it);\n            else\n                ++it;\n        }\n    }\n\nprivate:\n    IUserRepository&            m_userRepo;\n    IPasswordResetRepository&   m_tokenRepo;\n    IEmailDispatcher&           m_emailDispatcher;\n    Config                      m_cfg;\n\n    mutable std::mutex                               m_rateMutex;\n    std::unordered_map<std::string, RateInfo>        m_rateLog;\n};\n\n} // namespace intraledger::blogsuite::auth\n```",

      mu_;  // allows concurrent reads while writes are unique\n    std::list<std::pair<Key, Value>> list_;\n    std::unordered_map<Key, typename std::list<std::pair<Key, Value>>::iterator> map_;\n};\n\n// -----------------------------------------------------------------------------\n// Query Parser\n//            std::regex::icase);\n        std::smatch m;\n        std::string s = input_;\n        while (std::regex_search(s, m, re)) {\n            std::string tok = m.str(0);\n            if (tok == The thread exits when the object is\n     *  destructed.\n     */\n    void maintenanceLoop()\n    {\n        BLOGSUITE_LOG_DEBUG(\"RateLimiter maintenance thread started\");\n        while (true)\n   auto it = index_.find(key);\n        if (it == index_.end()) return std::nullopt;\n\n        // Move the accessed item to the front of the list to mark it most-recently-used.\n        lru_.splice(lru_.begin(), lru_, it->second);\n        return it->second->second;\n    }\n\n    // Insert or update.\n    void put(Key key, Value value)\n    {\n        std::unique_lock lock{ mutex_ std::string snippet = std::string(body_html.substr(snippet_start, snippet_end - snippet_start));\n\n        // Highlight occurrences up to max_highlights.\n        std::size_t highlights = 0;\n        const std::vector<std::string>& query_terms)\n    {\n        const Key key{ article_id, compute_query_hash(query_terms) };\n\n        if (auto cached = cache_.get(key); cached.has_value()) {\n            return *cached;\n        }\n\n        // Miss: generate.\n        std::string snippet = generator_.generate(body_html, query_terms);\n\n        cache_.put(key, snippet);\n        return     "content": "```cpp\n/***********************************************************************\n*  IntraLedger BlogSuite \u2013 module_39.cpp\n*\n*  Component: RBAC (Role-Based Access-Control) Permission Evaluator\n*  ---------------------------------------------------------------------\n*  This module belongs to the Security / Authorization layer of\n*  BlogSuite.  It is responsible for efficiently determining whether a\n*  user possesses a specific permission by combining role membership\n*  (fetched via Repository) with an in-memory, thread-safe cache that\n*  features automatic time-to-live (TTL) expiry.\n*\n*  NOTE:\n*    \u2022 This file is self-contained to keep example size reasonable; in\n*      production it would be split into separate headers/sources.\n*    \u2022 Any database access is simulated through an in-memory repository\n*      (see `InMemoryRoleRepository`) so the file builds standalone.\n*\n*  Author : IntraLedger Engineering\n*  License: Proprietary, All Rights Reserved\n***********************************************************************/\n\n#include <algorithm>\n#include <bitset>\n#include <chrono>\n#include <cstdint>\n#include <cstdlib>\n#include <future>\n#include <iostream>\n#include <memory>\n#include <mutex>\n#include <shared_mutex>\n#include <string>\n#include <thread>\n#include <unordered_map>\n#include <utility>\n#include <vector>\n\nnamespace ilbs   /* IntraLedger BlogSuite */\n{\nnamespace rbac   /* Role-Based Access Control */\n{\n\n/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */\n/* 1. Permission Enumeration                                           */\n/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */\n\nenum class Permission : std::uint16_t\n{\n    ReadArticle          = 0,\n    WriteArticle         = 1,\n    PublishArticle       = 2,\n    DeleteArticle        = 3,\n    ManageUsers          = 4,\n    ManageSubscriptions  = 5,\n    ViewAnalytics        = 6,\n    SystemAdministration = 7,\n\n    COUNT /* Keep this one last */\n};\n\nconstexpr std::size_t kPermissionCount =\n    static_cast<std::size_t>(Permission::COUNT);\n\n/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */\n/* 2. Role Entity                                                      */\n/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */\n\nstruct Role\n{\n    std::uint32_t      id             = 0;\n    std::string        name;\n    std::bitset<kPermissionCount> permissions;\n};\n\n/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */\n/* 3. Repository Interface & Mock Implementation                       */\n/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */\n\nclass IUserRoleRepository\n{\npublic:\n    virtual ~IUserRoleRepository() = default;\n    virtual std::vector<Role> fetchRolesForUser(std::uint32_t userId) = 0;\n};\n\n/*\n * A very small in-memory repository to simulate database calls.\n * Thread-safe and deliberately slow to help verify the cache path.\n */\nclass InMemoryRoleRepository final : public IUserRoleRepository\n{\npublic:\n    InMemoryRoleRepository()\n    {\n        // --- Seed demo roles ----------------------------------------\n        Role author;\n        author.id   = 1;\n        author.name = \"Author\";\n        author.permissions.set(static_cast<std::size_t>(Permission::ReadArticle));\n        author.permissions.set(static_cast<std::size_t>(Permission::WriteArticle));\n        author.permissions.set(static_cast<std::size_t>(Permission::PublishArticle));\n\n        Role admin;\n        admin.id   = 2;\n        admin.name = \"Administrator\";\n        admin.permissions.set(); // all bits to 1\n        admin.permissions.reset(static_cast<std::size_t>(Permission::DeleteArticle)); // Example\n\n        m_rolesByUser.emplace(1001U, std::vector<Role>{author});\n        m_rolesByUser.emplace(  42U, std::vector<Role>{author, admin});\n    }\n\n    std::vector<Role> fetchRolesForUser(std::uint32_t userId) override\n    {\n        // Simulate I/O latency\n        std::this_thread::sleep_for(std::chrono::milliseconds(25));\n\n        const auto it = m_rolesByUser.find(userId);\n        if (it == m_rolesByUser.end())\n            return {};\n\n        return it->second;\n    }\n\nprivate:\n    std::unordered_map<std::uint32_t, std::vector<Role>> m_rolesByUser;\n};\n\n/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */\n/* 4. Permission Evaluator Service                                     */\n/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */\n\nclass PermissionEvaluator\n{\npublic:\n    explicit PermissionEvaluator(std::shared_ptr<IUserRoleRepository> repo,\n                                 std::chrono::seconds cacheTtl = std::chrono::minutes(2))\n        : m_repo(std::move(repo)), m_cacheTtl(cacheTtl)\n    {\n        if (!m_repo)\n            throw std::invalid_argument(\"IUserRoleRepository cannot be null\");\n\n        // Schedule periodic cache pruning\n        m_cleanerThread = std::thread(&PermissionEvaluator::housekeepingWorker, this);\n    }\n\n    ~PermissionEvaluator()\n    {\n        m_shutdownRequested.store(true);\n        if (m_cleanerThread.joinable())\n            m_cleanerThread.join();\n    }\n\n    PermissionEvaluator(const PermissionEvaluator&)            = delete;\n    PermissionEvaluator& operator=(const PermissionEvaluator&) = delete;\n\n    /* Evaluate whether the user has `perm`. Fast path hits the cache. */\n    bool hasPermission(std::uint32_t userId, Permission perm)\n    {\n        const CacheKey key{userId, perm};\n\n        // ---------- 1. Try cache hit (shared lock) -----------------\n        {\n            std::shared_lock<std::shared_mutex> rLock(m_cacheMutex);\n            auto it = m_cache.find(key);\n            if (it != m_cache.end() && !isExpired(it->second))\n            {\n                return it->second.granted;\n            }\n        }\n\n        // ---------- 2. Slow path \u2011 fetch from repository -----------\n        bool granted = false;\n        try\n        {\n            // Launch fetch asynchronously to prevent blocking for too long\n            std::future<std::vector<Role>> fut =\n                std::async(std::launch::async, &IUserRoleRepository::fetchRolesForUser, m_repo, userId);\n\n            const std::vector<Role> roles = fut.get();\n            granted                       = evaluateRoles(roles, perm);\n        }\n        catch (const std::exception& ex)\n        {\n            // Log & fall back to conservative denial; in real code route to logger\n            std::cerr << \"[RBAC] Repository access failed: \" << ex.what() << '\\n';\n            granted = false;\n        }\n\n        // ---------- 3. Store in cache (unique lock) ----------------\n        {\n            std::unique_lock<std::shared_mutex> wLock(m_cacheMutex);\n            m_cache[key] = CacheEntry{granted, std::chrono::steady_clock::now()};\n        }\n\n        return granted;\n    }\n\n    /* Explicitly invalidate all cached permissions for a user. */\n    void invalidateUser(std::uint32_t userId)\n    {\n        std::unique_lock<std::shared_mutex> wLock(m_cacheMutex);\n        for (auto it = m_cache.begin(); it != m_cache.end();)\n        {\n            if (it->first.userId == userId)\n                it = m_cache.erase(it);\n            else\n                ++it;\n        }\n    }\n\nprivate:\n    /* --------------------- Internal Structures ------------------- */\n\n    struct CacheKey\n    {\n        std::uint32_t userId;\n        Permission    permission;\n\n        bool operator==(const CacheKey& other) const noexcept\n        {\n            return userId == other.userId && permission == other.permission;\n        }\n    };\n\n    struct CacheKeyHasher\n    {\n        std::size_t operator()(const CacheKey& k) const noexcept\n        {\n            return (static_cast<std::size_t>(k.userId) << 8) ^\n                   static_cast<std::size_t>(k.permission);\n        }\n    };\n\n    struct CacheEntry\n    {\n        bool granted;\n        std::chrono::steady_clock::time_point ts;\n    };\n\n    /* --------------------- Helper Utilities ---------------------- */\n\n    static bool evaluateRoles(const std::vector<Role>& roles, Permission perm)\n    {\n        const std::size_t index = static_cast<std::size_t>(perm);\n        return std::any_of(roles.begin(), roles.end(),\n                           [index](const Role& r) { return r.permissions.test(index); });\n    }\n\n    bool isExpired(const CacheEntry& e) const noexcept\n    {\n        return (std::chrono::steady_clock::now() - e.ts) > m_cacheTtl;\n    }\n\n    void housekeepingWorker()\n    {\n        using namespace std::chrono_literals;\n        while (!m_shutdownRequested.load())\n        {\n            {\n                std::unique_lock<std::shared_mutex> wLock(m_cacheMutex);\n                for (auto it = m_cache.begin(); it != m_cache.end();)\n                {\n                    if (isExpired(it->second))\n                        it = m_cache.erase(it);\n                    else\n                        ++it;\n                }\n            }\n            std::this_thread::sleep_for(15s);\n        }\n    }\n\n    /* --------------------- Data Members -------------------------- */\n\n    std::shared_ptr<IUserRoleRepository> m_repo;\n    std::chrono::seconds                 m_cacheTtl;\n\n    std::unordered_map<CacheKey, CacheEntry, CacheKeyHasher> m_cache;\n    mutable std::shared_mutex                                  m_cacheMutex;\n\n    std::thread                     m_cleanerThread;\n    std::atomic_bool                m_shutdownRequested{false};\n};\n\n/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */\n/* 5. Stand-Alone Test Harness                                         */\n/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */\n\n#if defined(ILBS_RBAC_UNIT_TEST)\n/*\n * A quick single-threaded functional check. Compile with:\n *   g++ -std=c++20 -DILBS_RBAC_UNIT_TEST module_39.cpp -lpthread\n */\nint main()\n{\n    using namespace ilbs::rbac;\n\n    auto repo     = std::make_shared<InMemoryRoleRepository>();\n    PermissionEvaluator evaluator(repo, std::chrono::seconds(10));\n\n    const std::uint32_t user = 1001;\n\n    std::cout << \"User \" << user << \" may publish? \"\n              << evaluator.hasPermission(user, Permission::PublishArticle) << '\\n';\n\n    std::cout << \"User \" << user << \" may delete?  \"\n              << evaluator.hasPermission(user, Permission::DeleteArticle) << '\\n';\n\n    // Invalidate and recheck (should force repo fetch again)\n    evaluator.invalidateUser(user);\n\n    std::cout << \"After invalidation: may publish? \"\n              << evaluator.hasPermission(user, Permission::PublishArticle) << '\\n';\n\n    return EXIT_SUCCESS;\n}\n#endif /* ILBS_RBAC_UNIT_TEST */\n\n} // namespace rbac\n} // namespace ilbs\n```",

std::string\n    highlightSnippet(std::string_view text, std::string_view queryTerm) {\n\n        if (text.empty() || queryTerm.empty()) { return {}; }\n\n        // Case-insensitive search\n        std::string hayStack{ text };\n        std::string needle{ queryTerm };\n        std::transform(hayStack.begin(), hayStack.end(), hayStack.begin(), ::tolower);\n        std::transform(needle.begin(), /*----------------------------------------------------\n     * constantTimeEquals\n     *\n     * Compares two byte sequences in constant time to\n     * mitigate timing attacks.\n It follows the classic\n *  \u201cvoter\u201d strategy found in many security frameworks (e.g., Spring Security)\n *  and adds a thread-safe, bounded LRU cache to avoid re-computing expensive\n * {\n        std::hash<std::string> h;\n        return (h(k.userId) ^ (h(k.resourceId) << 1)) ^ (h(k.action) << 2);\n    }\n};\n\n// <typename Key, typename Value, typename Hasher = std::hash<Key>>\nclass LRUCache\n{\npublic:\n    explicit LRUCache(std::size_t capacity)\n        : m_capacity(capacity)\n    {\n        if (capacity == 0)\n            throw std::invalid_argument(\"LRUCache capacity must be > 0\");\n    }\n\n    std::optional<Value> get(const Key& key)\n    {\n        std::unique_lock lock(m_mutex);\n        auto it = m_map.find(key);\n        if (it == m_map.end()) return std::nullopt;\n\n        // Move accessed element to front (most-recent)\n        m_list.splice(m_list.begin(), m_list, it->second);\n        return it->second->second;\n    }\n\n    void put(const Key& key, const Value& value)\n    {\n        std::unique_lock lock(m_mutex);\n\n        auto it = m_map.find(key);\n        if (it != m_map.end())\n        {\n            // Override existing entry\n            it->second->second = value;\n            m_list.splice(m_list.begin(), m_list, it->second);\n            return;\n        }\n\n        // Insert new entry\n        m_list.emplace_front(key, value);\n        m_map[key] = m_list.begin();\n\n        // Evict if needed\n        if (m_map.size() > m_capacity)\n        {\n            auto last = m_list.end();\n            --last;\n            m_map.erase(last->first);\n            m_list.pop_back();\n        }\n    }\n\nprivate:\n    using ListType = std::list<std::pair<Key, Value>>;\n\n    std::size_t                         m_capacity;\n    ListType                            m_list;\n    std::unordered_map<Key,\n                       typename ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n// Voter Interfaces\n// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\nclass IAccessVoter\n{\npublic:\n    virtual ~IAccessVoter() = default;\n\n    /*\n     * Return true if this voter grants permission for the action on\n     * the resource by the given user. A voter that is not applicable\n     * should return std::nullopt.\n     */\n    virtual std::optional<bool>\n    vote(const UserContext&       user,\n         const ResourceDescriptor res,\n         std::string_view         action) const = 0;\n\nprotected:\n    // helper for inheritors\n    static bool roleIn(const UserContext& user, Role r)\n    {\n        return user.hasRole(r);\n    }\n};\n\n// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n// Concrete Voters\n// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n// 1. Role-based voter --------------------------------------------------------\nclass RoleVoter final : public IAccessVoter\n{\npublic:\n    std::optional<bool>\n    vote(const UserContext& user,\n         const ResourceDescriptor /*res*/,\n         std::string_view action) const override\n    {\n        if (action == \"admin\")\n        {\n            // Only admins may perform \"admin\" actions\n            return roleIn(user, Role::Admin) || roleIn(user, Role::SuperAdmin);\n        }\n\n        // Non-admin actions are not this voter's responsibility\n        return std::nullopt;\n    }\n};\n\n// 2. Ownership voter ---------------------------------------------------------\nclass OwnershipVoter final : public IAccessVoter\n{\npublic:\n    std::optional<bool>\n    vote(const UserContext& user,\n         const ResourceDescriptor res,\n         std::string_view action) const override\n    {\n        if (action == \"edit\" || action == \"delete\")\n        {\n            return res.ownerId == user.id || roleIn(user, Role::Editor) || roleIn(user, Role::SuperAdmin);\n        }\n\n        return std::nullopt;\n    }\n};\n\n// 3. Visibility / subscription voter ----------------------------------------\nclass VisibilityVoter final : public IAccessVoter\n{\npublic:\n    std::optional<bool>\n    vote(const UserContext& user,\n         const ResourceDescriptor res,\n         std::string_view action) const override\n    {\n        if (action != \"read\")\n            return std::nullopt;\n\n        if (res.isPublic) return true;\n        if (!user.authenticated) return false;\n\n        // Pretend a repository call that certifies premium subscription.\n        // We replace it with simple role check for demo purposes.\n        return res.isPremium ? roleIn(user, Role::Reader) || roleIn(user, Role::Author) ||\n                                   roleIn(user, Role::Editor) || roleIn(user, Role::Admin) ||\n                                   roleIn(user, Role::SuperAdmin)\n                             : true;\n    }\n};\n\n// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n// Permission Service (Affirmative-Based Decision Manager)\n// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\nclass PermissionService\n{\npublic:\n    // Dependency injection (repositories, config, etc.)\n    struct Dependencies\n    {\n        std::shared_ptr<IUserRepository>        userRepo;\n        std::shared_ptr<IArticleRepository>     articleRepo;\n        std::shared_ptr<ISubscriptionRepository> subscriptionRepo;\n    };\n\n    explicit PermissionService(Dependencies deps,\n                               std::size_t    cacheSize = 4'096)\n        : m_deps(std::move(deps))\n        , m_cache(cacheSize)\n    {\n        // Register built-in voters\n        m_voters.emplace_back(std::make_unique<RoleVoter>());\n        m_voters.emplace_back(std::make_unique<OwnershipVoter>());\n        m_voters.emplace_back(std::make_unique<VisibilityVoter>());\n    }\n\n    /*\n     * Evaluate permission for a user/action/resource triple.\n     * An \"affirmative\" strategy is used: the first voter that\n     * returns true grants access, while explicit false denies.\n     * If no voter returns a result, deny by default.\n     */\n    bool hasPermission(const UserContext& user,\n                       const ResourceDescriptor& resource,\n                       std::string_view action)\n    {\n        // Check cache\n        PermissionKey key{user.id, resource.ownerId /* acts as resourceId */, std::string(action)};\n        if (auto cached = m_cache.get(key))\n            return *cached;\n\n        bool result = evaluate(user, resource, action);\n\n        // Store in cache\n        m_cache.put(key, result);\n        return result;\n    }\n\nprivate:\n    bool evaluate(const UserContext& user,\n                  const ResourceDescriptor& resource,\n                  std::string_view action) const\n    {\n        // SuperAdmin shortcut\n        if (user.hasRole(Role::SuperAdmin))\n            return true;\n\n        // Delegating to voters\n        for (const auto& voter : m_voters)\n        {\n            try\n            {\n                std::optional<bool> voteResult = voter->vote(user, resource, action);\n\n                if (!voteResult.has_value())\n                    continue; // abstain \u2011> next voter\n\n                if (*voteResult)\n                    return true;  // grant immediately\n\n                // deny overrides all\n                return false;\n            }\n            catch (const std::exception& e)\n            {\n                // Defensive: log & move on to next voter\n                std::cerr << \"[security] Voter exception: \" << e.what() << '\\n';\n            }\n        }\n\n        // No voter granted access, deny by default\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    Dependencies                                     m_deps;\n    std::vector<std::unique_ptr<IAccessVoter>>       m_voters;\n    LRUCache<PermissionKey, bool, PermissionKeyHasher> m_cache;\n};\n\n// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n// Simple inline unit test (can be excluded in production builds)\n// deps{/*nullptr, nullptr, nullptr*/};\n    PermissionService svc(deps, 32);\n\n    UserContext alice { \"alice\", {Role::Author}, true };\n    UserContext bob   { \"bob\",   {Role::Reader}, true };\n    UserContext admin { \"admin\", {Role::Admin},  true };\n\n    ResourceDescriptor pubArticle  { \"alice\", true,  false };\n    ResourceDescriptor privArticle { \"alice\", false, true  };\n\n    // Public read\n    assert( svc.hasPermission(bob, pubArticle, \"read\") );\n\n    // Private read w/o subscription -> deny\n    assert( !svc.hasPermission(bob, privArticle, \"read\") );\n\n    // Owner can edit\n    assert( svc.hasPermission(alice, pubArticle, \"edit\") );\n\n    // Non-owner cannot delete\n    assert( !svc.hasPermission(bob, pubArticle, \"delete\") );\n\n    // Admin can admin\n    assert( svc.hasPermission(admin, pubArticle, \"admin\") );\n\n    // Cache hit (repeat query)\n    assert( svc.hasPermission(admin, pubArticle, \"admin\") );\n}\n\nstatic int _ = (selfTest(), \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n// Analytics Aggregator \u2013 public API (Service Layer)\n// \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n\nnamespace ilb::service\n{\n\n/**\n * Thread-safe, process-wide singleton that collects raw page-view events\n * and flushes the aggregated counters to the persistence layer.\n *\n * Usage:\n *     AnalyticsAggregator::instance().recordView(tenantId, articleId, userId);\n */\nclass AnalyticsAggregator\n{\npublic:\n    // Non-copyable / Non-movable\n    AnalyticsAggregator(const AnalyticsAggregator&)            = delete;\n    AnalyticsAggregator& operator=(const AnalyticsAggregator&) = delete;\n    AnalyticsAggregator(AnalyticsAggregator&&)                 = delete;\n    AnalyticsAggregator& operator=(AnalyticsAggregator&&)      = delete;\n\n    static AnalyticsAggregator& instance()\n    {\n        static AnalyticsAggregator inst;\n        return inst;\n    }\n\n    ~AnalyticsAggregator()\n    {\n        shutdown();\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Records a page-view event. Extremely hot path; optimized for minimal\n     * contention via per-bucket sharding and atomic counters.\n     */\n    void recordView(std::int64_t tenantId, std::int64_t articleId, std::int64_t /*userId*/)\n    {\n        const Key key{tenantId, articleId};\n        auto& bucket = m_buckets[key % m_buckets.size()];\n\n        {\n            std::unique_lock lk(bucket.mutex);\n            ++bucket.map[key];\n        }\n\n        // Fast path: only wake the flusher when certain thresholds are met.\n        const auto current = ++m_eventCounter;\n        if (current >= m_flushThreshold)\n        {\n            std::lock_guard lg(m_flushMutex);\n            m_shouldFlush = true;\n            m_cvFlush.notify_one();\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Graceful shutdown \u2013 ensures all counters make it to persistent storage.\n     * Safe to call multiple times.\n     */\n    void shutdown()\n    {\n        bool expected = false;\n        if (!m_shutdown.compare_exchange_strong(expected, true)) return;\n\n        {\n            std::lock_guard lg(m_flushMutex);\n            m_shouldFlush = true;\n            m_cvFlush.notify_one();\n        }\n        if (m_flushThread.joinable()) m_flushThread.join();\n    }\n\nprivate:\n    // \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500 Types \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n    struct Key\n    {\n        std::int64_t tenantId;\n        std::int64_t articleId;\n\n        std::size_t operator%(std::size_t mod) const noexcept\n        {\n            // Simple mixing hash for bucket selection.\n            std::uint64_t h = static_cast<std::uint64_t>(tenantId) ^ (static_cast<std::uint64_t>(articleId) << 1);\n            return static_cast<std::size_t>(h % mod);\n        }\n\n        bool operator==(const Key& other) const noexcept\n        {\n            return tenantId == other.tenantId && articleId == other.articleId;\n        }\n    };\n\n    struct KeyHash\n    {\n        std::size_t operator()(const Key& k) const noexcept\n        {\n            return k.tenantId * 31ull ^ k.articleId;\n        }\n    };\n\n    using Map  = std::unordered_map<Key, std::uint64_t, KeyHash>;\n    using Pair = std::pair<Key, std::uint64_t>;\n\n    struct Bucket\n    {\n        Map             map;\n        std::mutex      mutex;\n    };\n\n    // \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500 Ctor (private) \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n    AnalyticsAggregator()\n        : m_flushThread(&AnalyticsAggregator::flushLoop, this)\n    {\n    }\n\n    // \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500 Flushing Logic \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n    void flushLoop()\n    {\n        auto nextWake = std::chrono::steady_clock::now() + m_flushInterval;\n        std::unique_lock lk(m_flushMutex);\n\n        while (!m_shutdown.load(std::memory_order_acquire))\n        {\n            m_cvFlush.wait_until(lk, nextWake, [this] { return m_shouldFlush || m_shutdown.load(); });\n            m_shouldFlush = false;\n            lk.unlock();\n\n            try\n            {\n                flushOnce();\n            }\n            catch (const std::exception& ex)\n            {\n                // Log and continue. In production use a proper logger.\n                std::cerr << \"[AnalyticsAggregator] flush failed: \" << ex.what() << '\\n';\n            }\n\n            nextWake = std::chrono::steady_clock::now() + m_flushInterval;\n            lk.lock();\n        }\n\n        // Final flush on shutdown\n        lk.unlock();\n        flushOnce();\n    }\n\n    void flushOnce()\n    {\n        // Move data out of buckets with minimal holding time.\n        std::vector<Pair> snapshot;\n        snapshot.reserve(m_eventCounter.load());\n\n        for (auto& bucket : m_buckets)\n        {\n            std::lock_guard lg(bucket.mutex);\n            for (auto& [k, v] : bucket.map)\n            {\n                snapshot.emplace_back(k, v);\n            }\n            bucket.map.clear();\n        }\n\n        if (snapshot.empty()) return;\n        m_eventCounter = 0;\n\n        // Aggregate duplicates (rare; only occurs if hash bucket collision across shards).\n        std::unordered_map<Key, std::uint64_t, KeyHash> aggregated;\n        aggregated.reserve(snapshot.size());\n        for (const auto& [k, v] : snapshot) aggregated[k] += v;\n\n        // Persist to DB\n        orm::DbSession session;\n        repository::AnalyticsRepository repo(session);\n\n        session.transactional([&](orm::DbSession& /*tx*/) {\n            std::vector<repository::AnalyticsUpdate> batch;\n            batch.reserve(aggregated.size());\n\n            for (const auto& [k, count] : aggregated)\n            {\n                batch.push_back({k.tenantId, k.articleId, count});\n                if (batch.size() >= m_dbBatchSize)\n                {\n                    repo.bulkIncrement(batch);\n                    batch.clear();\n                }\n            }\n            if (!batch.empty()) repo.bulkIncrement(batch);\n        });\n    }\n\n    // \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500 Data Members \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n    static constexpr std::size_t kShardCount   = 64;\n    static constexpr std::uint64_t kDefaultThreshold = 10'000;\n\n    std::array<Bucket, kShardCount>    m_buckets{};\n    std::atomic<std::uint64_t>         m_eventCounter{0};\n\n    const std::chrono::seconds         m_flushInterval{10};\n    const std::uint64_t                m_flushThreshold{kDefaultThreshold};\n    const std::size_t                  m_dbBatchSize{1'024};\n\n    std::atomic<bool>                  m_shutdown{false};\n    std::thread                        m_flushThread;\n    std::condition_variable            m_cvFlush;\n    std::mutex                         m_flushMutex;\n    bool                               m_shouldFlush{false};\n};\n\n}  // namespace ilb::service\n\n// \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n// Core Authentication Module: SecureTokenService (module_74.cpp)\n\n```cpp\n// File: /app/project/src/module_74.cpp\n// Lines: 146-259\n\nclass SecureTokenService\n{\npublic:\n    struct Config\n    {\n        std::string       secretKey;     // HMAC secret (binary safe)\n        Seconds           defaultTTL     = Seconds { 900 }; // 15 minutes\n        std::string       issuer         = \"IntraLedger-BlogSuite\";\n        std::size_t       randomBytes    = 16;  // Random nonce length\n    };\n\n    explicit SecureTokenService(Config config)\n        : cfg_(std::move(config))\n    {\n        if (cfg_.secretKey.empty())\n            throw std::invalid_argument(\"Secret key must not be empty\");\n    }\n\n    // Generates a compact, URL-safe token for an arbitrary user payload\n    std::string generateToken(Json userPayload,\n                              std::optional<Seconds> ttl = std::nullopt) const\n    {\n        const auto now = Clock::now();\n        const auto exp = now + (ttl ? *ttl : cfg_.defaultTTL);\n\n        userPayload[\"iss\"] = cfg_.issuer;\n        userPayload[\"iat\"] = std::chrono::duration_cast<Seconds>(\n                                 now.time_since_epoch()).count();\n        userPayload[\"exp\"] = std::chrono::duration_cast<Seconds>(\n                                 exp.time_since_epoch()).count();\n        userPayload[\"jti\"] = randomHex(cfg_.randomBytes);\n        // ... signature generation using HMAC-SHA256\n    }\n\n    // Checks integrity & validity, returns decoded payload\n    Json verifyToken(std::string_view token) const\n    {\n        // Verify signature using constant-time comparison\n        // Validate timestamps (exp, nbf claims)\n        // Return decoded JSON payload\n    }\n};\n```\n\n### 2. Session Management: PermissionService / UserContext (module_52.cpp)\n\n```cpp\n// File: /app/project/src/module_52.cpp\n// Lines: 51-69, 259-302\n\nenum class Role {\n    Reader,\n    Author,\n    Editor,\n    Admin,\n    SuperAdmin\n};\n\nstruct UserContext final\n{\n    std::string            id;\n    std::vector<Role>      roles;\n    bool                   authenticated{false};\n\n    bool hasRole(Role r) const noexcept\n    {\n        return std::find(roles.begin(), roles.end(), r) != roles.end();\n    }\n};\n\nclass PermissionService\n{\npublic:\n    bool hasPermission(const UserContext& user,\n                       const ResourceDescriptor& resource,\n                       std::string_view action)\n    {\n        // Check cache\n        PermissionKey key{user.id, resource.ownerId, std::string(action)};\n        if (auto cached = m_cache.get(key))\n            return *cached;\n\n        bool result = evaluate(user, resource, action);\n        m_cache.put(key, result);\n        return result;\n    }\n};\n```\n\n### 3. Password Reset Workflow (module_56.cpp)\n\n```cpp\n// File: /app/project/src/module_56.cpp\n// Lines: 116-201\n\nclass PasswordResetService final\n{\npublic:\n    void requestPasswordReset(std::string_view email)\n    {\n        validateEmail(email);\n        // Rate limiting check\n        // Generate secure token\n        const auto token = generateToken();\n        // Persist token with expiry\n        m_tokenRepo.upsertToken(token, {\n            std::string{email},\n            now + m_cfg.tokenLifetime\n        });\n        // Dispatch email asynchronously\n        m_emailDispatcher.enqueueResetEmail(email, url.str());\n    }\n\n    void resetPassword(std::string_view token, std::string_view newPasswordHash)\n    {\n        auto record = m_tokenRepo.findToken(token);\n        if (!record)\n            throw TokenInvalid{\"Password-reset token invalid.\"};\n        if (now > record->expiresAt)\n            throw TokenExpired{\"Password-reset token expired.\"};\n\n        m_userRepo.updatePassword(record->email, newPasswordHash);\n        m_tokenRepo.removeToken(token);\n    }\n};\n```\n\n### 4.
