RBAC Permission Evaluator (module_39.cpp)\n\n```cpp\n// File: /app/project/src/module_39.cpp\n// Lines: 134-198\n\nclass PermissionEvaluator\n{\npublic:\n    explicit PermissionEvaluator(std::shared_ptr<IUserRoleRepository> repo,\n                                 std::chrono::seconds cacheTtl = std::chrono::minutes(2))\n\n    bool hasPermission(std::uint32_t userId, Permission perm)\n    {\n        // Cache check (shared lock)\n        // Slow path: fetch from repository\n        std::future<std::vector<Role>> fut =\n            std::async(std::launch::async, &IUserRoleRepository::fetchRolesForUser, m_repo, userId);\n\n        const std::vector<Role> roles = fut.get();\n        granted = evaluateRoles(roles, perm);\n        // Store in cache (unique lock)\n        return granted;\n    }\n\n    void invalidateUser(std::uint32_t userId);\n};\n```\n\n## Analysis\n\n### 1. Core Component Identification\n\nAfter thorough analysis of the IntraLedger BlogSuite codebase, I have identified the following **primary authentication and session management components**:\n\n#### Primary Authentication Modules:\n\n| Module | Class/Service | Purpose |\n|--------|---------------|---------|\n| **module_74.cpp** | `SecureTokenService` | **Core token management** - JWT-like token generation/validation using HMAC-SHA256 with OpenSSL. Handles all token-based authentication (password resets, email confirmations, OAuth state). |\n| **module_56.cpp** | `PasswordResetService` | **Password reset workflow** - Secure password reset with cryptographic token generation, rate limiting, and email dispatch. |\n| **module_52.cpp** | `PermissionService` | **Authorization gateway** - Central permission evaluation using voter pattern with LRU cache. Defines `UserContext` (the user session representation). |\n\n#### Supporting Authentication Modules:\n\n| Module | Class/Service | Purpose |\n|--------|---------------|---------|\n| **module_39.cpp** | `PermissionEvaluator` | RBAC-based permission evaluation with role membership caching |\n| **module_33.cpp** | `LoginAttemptThrottler` | Login attempt rate limiting and brute-force protection |\n| **module_46.cpp** | `TokenBucketRateLimiter` | Token-bucket rate limiter for login endpoints |\n| **module_11.cpp** | `AdaptiveRateLimiter` | Pluggable rate limiting with Redis/Memcached extension points |\n\n**Note:** The task description mentioned modules 12 and 35 as authentication modules, but analysis reveals these are actually **search modules** (SearchService and related query parsing). The actual authentication core is in modules 74, 56, and 52.\n\n### 2. Dependency Mapping\n\nThe following modules are **directly coupled** to the authentication/session components:\n\n| Dependent Module | Dependency Type | Nature of Coupling |\n|-----------------|-----------------|---------------------|\n| **module_64.cpp** (SearchService) | Uses `UserContext` | Requires `middleware::UserContext` to perform ACL-based filtering of search results via `userCtx.mayReadArticle(hit.articleId)` |\n| **module_66.cpp** (ContentMetricsService) | Uses `UserContext` | Depends on `UserContext.id` and `UserContext.ipAddress` for view deduplication and analytics tracking |\n| **module_76.cpp** (ScheduledPublicationService) | Uses `SessionFactory` | Requires ORM session factory for database transactions (different from user sessions) |\n| **module_39.cpp** (PermissionEvaluator) | Uses `IUserRoleRepository` | Fetches role memberships for permission evaluation, tightly coupled to the authorization subsystem |\n| **module_33.cpp** (LoginAttemptThrottler) | Rate-limits logins | Core authentication infrastructure - tracks failed/successful login attempts |\n| **module_46.cpp** (TokenBucketRateLimiter) | Rate-limits logins | Provides `isLoginAttemptAllowed()` API consumed by authentication middleware |\n| **module_56.cpp** (PasswordResetService) | Uses `IUserRepository`, `IEmailDispatcher` | Depends on user repository for password updates and email dispatcher for reset notifications |\n\n### 3. Key Architectural Observations\n\n1. **UserContext as the Session Representation**: The `UserContext` struct (defined in module_52.cpp and module_66.cpp) serves as the primary session representation, containing user ID, roles, and authentication status.\n\n2. **Token-Based Authentication**: The `SecureTokenService` in module_74.cpp implements JWT-like tokens using HMAC-SHA256, providing the foundation for stateless authentication.\n\n3. **Voter-Based Authorization**: The `PermissionService` uses a voter pattern (similar to Spring Security) where multiple voters (`RoleVoter`, `OwnershipVoter`, `VisibilityVoter`) contribute to access decisions.\n\n4. **Layered Rate Limiting**: Multiple rate limiting implementations exist:\n   - `LoginAttemptThrottler` - Per-user and per-IP rate limiting with database persistence\n   - `TokenBucketRateLimiter` - Process-wide singleton for login rate limiting\n   - `AdaptiveRateLimiter` - Pluggable backend with Redis support\n\n## Decoupling Strategy\n\n### Proposed Architecture: Abstract Authentication Interface (IAuthService)\n\nTo extract the authentication logic into a standalone SSO service while minimizing changes to dependent modules, I propose introducing an **abstract interface** following the **Dependency Inversion Principle**.\n\n#### 1. Define the IAuthService Interface\n\n```cpp\n// File: include/auth/IAuthService.hpp\n\nnamespace intraledger::auth {\n\n// Result types for authentication operations\nstruct AuthResult {\n    bool success;\n    std::optional<UserContext> userContext;\n    std::optional<std::string> errorMessage;\n};\n\nstruct TokenValidationResult {\n    bool valid;\n    std::optional<std::string> userId;\n    std::optional<std::vector<Role>> roles;\n    std::chrono::system_clock::time_point expiresAt;\n};\n\n// Abstract interface for authentication services\nclass IAuthService {\npublic:\n    virtual ~IAuthService() = default;\n\n    // Token operations\n    virtual std::string generateToken(const UserContext& user,\n                                      std::chrono::seconds ttl = std::chrono::seconds{900}) = 0;\n    virtual TokenValidationResult validateToken(std::string_view token) = 0;\n    virtual void revokeToken(std::string_view token) = 0;\n\n    // Session operations\n    virtual std::optional<UserContext> getSession(std::string_view sessionId) = 0;\n    virtual void invalidateSession(std::string_view sessionId) = 0;\n\n    // User authentication\n    virtual AuthResult authenticate(std::string_view username,\n                                    std::string_view passwordHash) = 0;\n\n    // Rate limiting\n    virtual bool isLoginAttemptAllowed(std::string_view clientKey) = 0;\n    virtual void recordLoginFailure(std::string_view clientKey) = 0;\n    virtual void recordLoginSuccess(std::string_view clientKey) = 0;\n};\n\n} // namespace intraledger::auth\n```\n\n#### 2. Create Local Implementation (Current Monolith)\n\n```cpp\n// File: src/auth/LocalAuthService.hpp\n\nclass LocalAuthService final : public IAuthService {\npublic:\n    LocalAuthService(std::shared_ptr<SecureTokenService> tokenService,\n                     std::shared_ptr<PermissionService> permissionService,\n                     std::shared_ptr<LoginAttemptThrottler> throttler)\n        : m_tokenService(std::move(tokenService))\n        , m_permissionService(std::move(permissionService))\n        , m_throttler(std::move(throttler))\n    {}\n\n    // Delegate to existing implementations\n    std::string generateToken(const UserContext& user, std::chrono::seconds ttl) override {\n        nlohmann::json payload = {{\"uid\", user.id}, {\"roles\", serializeRoles(user.roles)}};\n        return m_tokenService->generateToken(payload, ttl);\n    }\n\n    TokenValidationResult validateToken(std::string_view token) override {\n        try {\n            auto payload = m_tokenService->verifyToken(token);\n            return {true, payload[\"uid\"], deserializeRoles(payload[\"roles\"]),\n                    extractExpiry(payload)};\n        } catch (const TokenError&) {\n            return {false, std::nullopt, std::nullopt, {}};\n        }\n    }\n    // ... other method implementations\n};\n```\n\n#### 3. Create Remote SSO Implementation (Future)\n\n```cpp\n// File: src/auth/RemoteSSOService.hpp\n\nclass RemoteSSOService final : public IAuthService {\npublic:\n    RemoteSSOService(std::string ssoEndpoint,\n                     std::shared_ptr<HttpClient> httpClient)\n        : m_ssoEndpoint(std::move(ssoEndpoint))\n        , m_httpClient(std::move(httpClient))\n    {}\n\n    TokenValidationResult validateToken(std::string_view token) override {\n        auto response = m_httpClient->post(\n            m_ssoEndpoint + \"/api/v1/token/validate\",\n            {{\"token\", std::string(token)}}\n        );\n\n        if (response.status == 200) {\n            auto json = nlohmann::json::parse(response.body);\n            return {true, json[\"userId\"], parseRoles(json[\"roles\"]),\n                    parseExpiry(json[\"expiresAt\"])};\n        }\n        return {false, std::nullopt, std::nullopt, {}};\n    }\n    // ... other method implementations\n};\n```\n\n#### 4. Update Dependent Modules\n\nRefactor dependent modules to use the `IAuthService` interface:\n\n```cpp\n// Before (module_64.cpp - SearchService)\nclass SearchService {\npublic:\n    std::vector<SearchResult> search(std::string_view query,\n                                     const middleware::UserContext& userCtx,\n                                     std::size_t limit) const {\n        // Direct access to UserContext\n        if (!userCtx.mayReadArticle(hit.articleId)) { continue; }\n    }\n};\n\n// After\nclass SearchService {\npublic:\n    SearchService(std::shared_ptr<IAuthService> authService,\n                  std::shared_ptr<persistence::ArticleRepository> repo,\n                  std::shared_ptr<search::ISearchEngine> engine)\n        : m_authService(std::move(authService))\n        // ...\n    {}\n\n    std::vector<SearchResult> search(std::string_view query,\n                                     std::string_view sessionToken,\n                                     std::size_t limit) const {\n        auto validationResult = m_authService->validateToken(sessionToken);\n        if (!validationResult.valid) {\n            throw UnauthorizedException{};\n        }\n\n        // Create UserContext from token claims\n        UserContext userCtx{validationResult.userId.value(),\n                           validationResult.roles.value_or({}), true};\n\n        // Continue with existing logic\n    }\n};\n```\n\n### Migration Strategy\n\n1. **Phase 1 - Interface Introduction**: Add `IAuthService` interface and `LocalAuthService` implementation that wraps existing modules. No behavioral changes.\n\n2. **Phase 2 - Dependency Injection**: Update all dependent modules to accept `IAuthService` via constructor injection instead of direct dependencies.\n\n3. **Phase 3 - Configuration-Based Selection**: Implement factory/DI container configuration to select between `LocalAuthService` and `RemoteSSOService` based on environment.\n\n4. **Phase 4 - SSO Service Extraction**: Deploy the standalone SSO service and switch production configuration to use `RemoteSSOService`.\n\n### Benefits of This Approach\n\n1. **Dependency Inversion**: Application depends on abstraction (`IAuthService`), not concrete implementations\n2. **Minimal Code Changes**: Existing modules require only constructor signature changes\n3. **Testability**: Easy to mock `IAuthService` for unit testing\n4. **Gradual Migration**: Can switch implementations per-environment without code changes\n5. **Backward Compatibility**: `LocalAuthService` preserves existing behavior during transition\n\n## Summary\n\n- **Primary finding**: The core authentication system consists of **module_74.cpp (SecureTokenService)**, **module_56.cpp (PasswordResetService)**, and **module_52.cpp (PermissionService)** - not modules 12/35 as initially suggested (those are search modules).\n\n- **Key components**:\n  - `SecureTokenService` - JWT-like token generation/validation with HMAC-SHA256\n  - `PermissionService` - Voter-based authorization with LRU caching\n  - `PasswordResetService` - Secure password reset workflow\n  - `LoginAttemptThrottler` / `TokenBucketRateLimiter` - Rate limiting infrastructure\n  - `UserContext` - Session representation containing user ID, roles, and auth status\n\n- **Architectural pattern**: The recommended decoupling strategy uses the **Dependency Inversion Principle** with an **abstract IAuthService interface**, allowing transparent switching between local implementation and remote SSO service.\n\n- **Recommendations**:\n  1. Introduce `IAuthService` interface as the authentication contract\n  2. Create `LocalAuthService` wrapper for existing implementations\n  3. Update dependent modules to use dependency injection\n  4. Implement `RemoteSSOService` for SSO integration\n  5. Use configuration-based selection for gradual migration\n",

Session Management: PermissionService / UserContext (module_52.cpp)\n\n```cpp\n// File: /app/project/src/module_52.cpp\n// Lines: 51-69, 259-302\n\nenum class Role {\n    Reader,\n    Author,\n    Editor,\n    Admin,\n    SuperAdmin\n};\n\nstruct UserContext final\n{\n    std::string            id;\n    std::vector<Role>      roles;\n    bool                   authenticated{false};\n\n    bool hasRole(Role r) const noexcept\n    {\n        return std::find(roles.begin(), roles.end(), r) != roles.end();\n    }\n};\n\nclass PermissionService\n{\npublic:\n    bool hasPermission(const UserContext& user,\n                       const ResourceDescriptor& resource,\n                       std::string_view action)\n    {\n        // Check cache\n        PermissionKey key{user.id, resource.ownerId, std::string(action)};\n        if (auto cached = m_cache.get(key))\n            return *cached;\n\n        bool result = evaluate(user, resource, action);\n        m_cache.put(key, result);\n        return result;\n    }\n};\n```\n\n### 3. Password Reset Workflow (module_56.cpp)\n\n```cpp\n// File: /app/project/src/module_56.cpp\n// Lines: 116-201\n\nclass PasswordResetService final\n{\npublic:\n    void requestPasswordReset(std::string_view email)\n    {\n        validateEmail(email);\n        // Rate limiting check\n        // Generate secure token\n        const auto token = generateToken();\n        // Persist token with expiry\n        m_tokenRepo.upsertToken(token, {\n            std::string{email},\n            now + m_cfg.tokenLifetime\n        });\n        // Dispatch email asynchronously\n        m_emailDispatcher.enqueueResetEmail(email, url.str());\n    }\n\n    void resetPassword(std::string_view token, std::string_view newPasswordHash)\n    {\n        auto record = m_tokenRepo.findToken(token);\n        if (!record)\n            throw TokenInvalid{\"Password-reset token invalid.\"};\n        if (now > record->expiresAt)\n            throw TokenExpired{\"Password-reset token expired.\"};\n\n        m_userRepo.updatePassword(record->email, newPasswordHash);\n        m_tokenRepo.removeToken(token);\n    }\n};\n```\n\n### 4. Define the IAuthService Interface\n\n```cpp\n// File: include/auth/IAuthService.hpp\n\nnamespace intraledger::auth {\n\n// Result types for authentication operations\nstruct AuthResult {\n    bool success;\n    std::optional<UserContext> userContext;\n    std::optional<std::string> errorMessage;\n};\n\nstruct TokenValidationResult {\n    bool valid;\n    std::optional<std::string> userId;\n    std::optional<std::vector<Role>> roles;\n    std::chrono::system_clock::time_point expiresAt;\n};\n\n// Abstract interface for authentication services\nclass IAuthService {\npublic:\n    virtual ~IAuthService() = default;\n\n    // Token operations\n    virtual std::string generateToken(const UserContext& user,\n                                      std::chrono::seconds ttl = std::chrono::seconds{900}) = 0;\n    virtual TokenValidationResult validateToken(std::string_view token) = 0;\n    virtual void revokeToken(std::string_view token) = 0;\n\n    // Session operations\n    virtual std::optional<UserContext> getSession(std::string_view sessionId) = 0;\n    virtual void invalidateSession(std::string_view sessionId) = 0;\n\n    // User authentication\n    virtual AuthResult authenticate(std::string_view username,\n                                    std::string_view passwordHash) = 0;\n\n    // Rate limiting\n    virtual bool isLoginAttemptAllowed(std::string_view clientKey) = 0;\n    virtual void recordLoginFailure(std::string_view clientKey) = 0;\n    virtual void recordLoginSuccess(std::string_view clientKey) = 0;\n};\n\n} // namespace intraledger::auth\n```\n\n#### 2. # Solution: cpp_web_blog_expert_040_architectural_understanding_expert_01

## Architectural Analysis for Decoupling the Authentication Service in IntraLedger BlogSuite

## Key Files Identified

### Core Authentication and Session Management Components

- `/app/project/src/module_74.cpp` - **SecureTokenService**: Core token generation and validation using HMAC-SHA256, handles JWT-like tokens for authentication middleware (password resets, email confirmations, OAuth state)
- `/app/project/src/module_56.cpp` - **PasswordResetService**: Secure password reset workflow with rate-limiting, token generation, and email dispatch
- `/app/project/src/module_52.cpp` - **PermissionService**: Centralized permission-evaluation using voter architecture with LRU cache for authorization decisions
- `/app/project/src/module_39.cpp` - **RBAC PermissionEvaluator**: Role-based access control permission evaluator with TTL-based caching
- `/app/project/src/module_33.cpp` - **LoginAttemptThrottler**: Rate-limiting for login attempts to prevent brute-force attacks
- `/app/project/src/module_46.cpp` - **TokenBucketRateLimiter**: Token-bucket based rate limiter for login endpoints
- `/app/project/src/module_11.cpp` - **AdaptiveRateLimiter**: Production-grade rate limiting with pluggable backend storage

### Supporting Security Infrastructure

- `/app/project/src/utils.cpp` - Utility functions including `uuid_v4()` for secure token generation, email validation
- `/app/project/src/module_7.cpp` - **SessionFactory** / **Session**: ORM session management (database session, not user session)

### Modules with Authentication Dependencies

- `/app/project/src/module_64.cpp` - **SearchService**: Depends on `middleware::UserContext` for ACL-based filtering
- `/app/project/src/module_66.cpp` - **ContentMetri
... (truncated)
